\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{putStringList()}{putStringList()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void org.\+jabref.\+preferences.\+Jab\+Ref\+Preferences.\+put\+String\+List (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String}]{key,  }\item[{List$<$ String $>$}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Puts a list of strings into the Preferences, by linking its elements with a S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+L\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+I\+M\+I\+T\+ER into a single string. Escape characters make the process transparent even if strings contains a S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+L\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+I\+M\+I\+T\+ER. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classorg_1_1jabref_1_1preferences_1_1_jab_ref_preferences_aed5389f1b0a3aa0b53007cbc356a3dc2}\label{classorg_1_1jabref_1_1preferences_1_1_jab_ref_preferences_aed5389f1b0a3aa0b53007cbc356a3dc2}}
